General Information

• Rates may change without prior notice. Please contact our Front Desk/ Reception for latest rates

• Patients are expected to deposit 100% of estimated amount of surgery at the time of admission
•  Patients for medical admission are expected to maintain a positive balance of payments
during the course of Hospitalisation.
• The Prices would be charged as per the charges prevailing in the system on the day of admission.
• Please confirm availability of services from the Guest Relation Executive to
avoid inconvenience

• All promotional and economy packages / treatments are cash only

• No two or more promotional schemes can be clubbed together

• Discounts under different schemes or policies cannot be clubbed together

• One time Patient Registration charges Rs. 275/-
• MRD Charges of Rs. 850/- apply for each admission
• Sterilization Charges of Rs. 350/- are applicable for every stay
• Admission Charges of Rs. 800/- are applicable for every admission
• 5% service charge is applicable on all IP services, special instruments, OT equipment
and non-cardiac packages.
• Emergency visit policy is applicable from 8PM to 8AM

OPD Consultation

S. No. Type Rate
1 Directors & Senior Consultants 800 -2500
2 Consultants 500 - 1500
3 Associate Consultants / Jr. Consultants 200 - 800
4 Registrar 200 - 400
5 Dietician 300 - 700

IPD Policy

Consulting doctors are expected to make a minimum of one visit per day. If the
patient condition warrants more than 2 visits the same shall be given without extra
cost. Referral visits are extra.

Room Charge

• All discharges to follow the 12-noon 24-hour cycle.
• Admission duration of more than 6 hours in any billing cycle shall be charged for full day.
• Admission duration of less than 6 hours will incur a half day charge.
• Any patient who leaves the room within 2 hours of admission will not be charged
• Day care charges will be Rs.1000 for 4 hour
• In transfer of patients after 6hours the billing shall be done as per higher bill category
• Nursing charges as per room category are applicable.
• RMO charges as per room category are applicable

shall be Applicable as per higher room charges from the first day of
admission

OT Billing Policy

1. OT Charges

  OT Charges shall be 105% of the Surgeon fee / Procedure charges. 
 OT Charges shall be calculated based on the net procedure price as applicable. 

2. Anaesthesiology Charges

 Anaesthesia will be charged as per the type of anaesthesia given to patient. 

S. No. Heads Rate

1 General Anaesthesia 40%
2 Spinal / Epidural 40%
3 Regional Anaesthesia 40%
4 Local Anaesthesia 20%
5 Standby Anaesthesia 25%

• Anaesthesia charges shall be calculated based on the net procedure price as applicable
(in case of high risk, emergency, re-exploration, staged surgeries , etc. ).

• If a surgeon requires that local Anaesthesia / Sedation be monitored by Anaesthetist,
then the charge for the same will be 15% of the procedure charges.

• In case procedures are done under different types of anaesthesia, charges shall be
levied on each procedure independently.

• If Anaesthetist is used during MRI, the charges for Anaesthetist are Rs. 1000/- a part
from MRI Charges

3. Surgeon Fee

  Surgeon fee shall be charged as per room category. 
 Two surgeries done by same Doctor or two doctors in the same incision then
 main Procedure will be charged full & sub procedure will be charged at 50% 
  Two different procedures done in two different incisions by two different doctors or
a single doctor the procedure charge shall be 100% 

Page 11 of 152
2022 Tariff

 If procedures are done on two different days during the same hospitalisation then
 there shall be 100% charges for each procedure 
 Re-exploration after two days of surgery shall be charged at 50%. 

 Second Surgery will be at 50% and third surgery at 25%. 

 Assistant Surgeon fee will be at 25% of the total surgeon fee. 

4. Packages

 First / Main package will be charged full and sub procedure cost will be charged on
actual –100% of Surgeon’s Fees if done on a different incision and 50% on surgeon’s
fees if on the same incision. OT &Anaesthesia charges will be made on the actual
surgeon’s fees for these procedures 

5. General Policy for Packages:

• All Promotional / Economy packages are cash payment basis only.
• For all planned surgical / interventional cases, 100% of estimated cost has to be
deposited prior to OT.
• Package-day is only for a given number of admission days. Normal charges shall be
applied after the end of package period.
• All medication of a pre-existing disease shall be out of the package. For example
Insulin, Thyroxin etc.
• Any higher anti-biotic used for treatment shall be extra.
• Consultation, procedure and investigation not related to the medical condition shall be
charged extra.
• All implants are extra.
• All packages start from the day of Surgery.

Note: 5% Service charge applicable on all services and non-cardiac packages.
